{\n            d.pitfallEvents.push(pe);\n          }\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  });\n  if (n > 0) {\n    showToast(n + ' treatment order(s) submitted', 'success');\n    saveState();\n The patient literally gets better (or worse) based on what you order.\n\n**Pitfall Events** \u2014 ordering insulin without D50 triggers a hypoglycemia crisis. Giving a saline bolus triggers worsening pulmonary edema. Each shows the adverse event, the clinical consequence, and the recovery teaching.\n\n**localStorage Persistence** \u2014 auto-saves after every chat, lab order, imaging order, and treatment. Sessions less than 4 hours old auto-resume on page load. Older sessions show a \"Resume Session\" button.
